              .          .         .                      .                      .                  .                  .                 .                 .                     .                   .          .   .      // Cost: O(nnz) conversion, done once here, amortized over all CG iterations.

            .         .         .                  .                 .                 .                   .                 .                  .                   .                 .         .   .      // there is no special optimization
